<h3 class="wp-block-heading">The Healing History of Copper</h3>
<p>Copper is one of the oldest metals known to humanity—used for over <strong>10,000 years</strong>. Ancient civilizations such as the <strong>Egyptians, Greeks, Romans, and Indians</strong> recognized its powerful <strong>healing and protective properties</strong> long before modern science confirmed its benefits.</p>
<p>The <strong>Ancient Egyptians</strong> used copper to <strong>sterilize wounds</strong> and purify drinking water. In <strong>Ayurvedic medicine</strong>, copper water vessels were used to balance the body&#8217;s <strong>three doshas</strong> (Vata, Pitta, and Kapha) and promote overall wellness. The <strong>Greeks and Romans</strong> used copper salves to treat <strong>skin conditions and inflammation</strong>, while wearing copper jewelry to support <strong>circulation, pain relief, and energy balance</strong>. Custom Copper Healing Tools Order Direct |Copper Collections</p>
<p>In modern times, copper continues to be valued for its <strong>antimicrobial, anti-inflammatory, and conductive</strong> properties. As a natural conductor of energy, copper is believed to <strong>enhance the flow of life force (chi or prana)</strong> throughout the body. It is commonly used in <strong>energy healing</strong>, <strong>spiritual practices</strong>, and <strong>EMF protection</strong>. Custom Copper Healing Tools Order Direct |Copper Collections</p>
<p>At <strong>Copper Collections</strong>, we honor this ancient wisdom by crafting tools and jewelry that harness copper’s natural ability to support <strong>healing, grounding, and energetic balance</strong>.</p>
